                    [32m'      --ignore-working-copy\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"          Don't snapshot the working copy, and don't update it\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'          \r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'          By default, Jujutsu snapshots the working copy at the beginning of every command. The\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'          working copy is also updated at the end of the command, if the command modified the\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'          working-copy commit (`@`). If you want to avoid snapshotting the working copy and instead\r\n'[39m +
